Important News Two

Liu Xiang Requests Construction of the Yuqin Railway

Army Commander Liu Xiang telegraphed the Ministry of Railways some months ago, requesting the construction of the Yuqin Railway. The original telegram stated the reasons for the urgent need to construct the road, which were highly valued. It is recorded as follows: "Minister of Railways Sun Zhesheng, esteemed brother, Having recently read the proposal for the road construction plan using the Gengzi and Guanshui indemnities, and having met with the special envoy of your ministry, Ding Zaijun, the head of the Southwest Geological Survey Team, and Chen Yanguang and Zeng Kejia, members of the Yunnan-Guizhou-Guangxi Economic Survey Committee, I am delighted to learn that the central government is following the Premier's industrial plan and will use the Gengzi and Guanshui indemnities to construct the Xiangdian Railway and the Yuedian Railway, and is planning the Yuqin branch line on the Xiangdian line and the Yuliu branch line on the Yuedian line. This shows profound foresight and a grand scale. I deeply admire and look up to it. However, I have found that Sichuan is an important southwestern town with a large population and vast territory, abundant in resources. Various mineral deposits such as non-ferrous metals, coal, iron, rock salt, and petroleum are found everywhere. The southwestern part of Sichuan is close to the Kangzang mountains, which are extremely rich in mineral resources. The British have long coveted this area and have already built a branch line from the Calcutta on the main trunk road of northern India, directly to Darjeeling in Sikkim, as a passage from India to Tibet. Russia is also planning to advance further from the Central Asian Railway, penetrating our country's Xinjiang territory and connecting to southern Tibet to spy on India. Border defense is becoming increasingly urgent, and the nation's lifeline is tightening. Furthermore, for the sake of developing and facilitating the economy, politics, and national defense of the Southwest, it is appropriate to urgently catch up and construct. Xiangbo visited with arguments, and through observation, I would like to slightly modify the general plan and suggest first building the Yuqin Railway as the backbone, with the Xiangdian and Yuedian lines as its parallels. I would like to briefly explain the reasoning. The Yuqin line connects the Chengdu-Chongqing Railway, running horizontally through the administrative provincial capitals of Sichuan, Guizhou, and Guangxi, which is suitable for connecting the southwestern interior trunk line and controlling politics. It also has the advantage of transporting products to the sea. That is the first advantage. The Beihai fortress has railways to connect and respond to each other. It has the advantage of unobstructed communication. That will definitely strengthen national defense. Furthermore, Beihai is owned by our country and is not like Hong Kong and Haiphong, which are under the spheres of influence of the British and French, and have no room for development. It is truly the only tool for developing agriculture, industry, and commerce. That is the second advantage. By running through Sichuan, Guizhou, and Guangxi provinces to the sea, the three provinces will share benefits. That way, Guizhou and Guangxi provinces will no longer have the problem of competing to build the Xiangdian and Yuedian lines, and the vast Sichuan will also avoid partial neglect. That is the third advantage. The Yuedian line is 1,300 miles long and requires a construction cost of 160 million yuan. The Xiangdian line is 1,100 miles long and requires a construction cost of 150 million yuan. The Saqin and Yuliu lines have not yet been calculated. According to recent surveys, the Yuqin line is only about 100 miles long and requires a cost of about 100 million yuan. The route has been surveyed from Chongqing through Qijiang, Songkan, Tongzi, Zunyi, Guiyang, Dushan, Nandan, Hechi, Qingyuan, Qianjiang, Nanning, and to Qinzhou Bay. The slope is not large, so the cost is saved and the construction is easy. That is the fourth advantage. After the Yuqin Railway is built, gradually build from Changsha to Guiyang or from Guiyang to Kunming, and from Guangzhou Sanshui to Qianjiang or from Kunming to Qianjiang. Consider financial resources, divide the work, and implement it simultaneously. Each segment has the effect of one segment. That is the fifth advantage. Now the Yuqi highway has already started, and the highway from Wenshui to Guiyang has also been opened to traffic. The highway project from Guiyang to Guilin is also about to be completed. For the Yuqin Railway, the foundation is already roughly in place. It is easier to succeed if construction is carried out in a timely manner. That is the sixth advantage. Sichuan's products, population, and land area are many times greater than those of Yunnan, Guizhou, Guangxi, and Guangdong provinces. The port of Beihai is freely managed by the government and is fully controlled, which is sufficient to promote the reclamation and immigration of the Southwest, to benefit the rural economy, and to inspire mineral deposits, supplement the skewed and dilapidated economy of the Southwest, and move towards industrialization. At the same time, the business of this road can be comparable to Longhai and Jinpu, which is sufficient to enrich the national treasury's income. That is the seventh advantage. After the Yuqin Railway is built, the Chengdu-Kangding Railway can be built with the income from its business, and the Ningjing-Changdu railway can be built via Kangding Yajiang to Qianzang to Lhasa, crossing the Yarlung Tsangpo River and reaching Yadongguan, connecting with the British Darjeeling-Calcutta railways, which will open up the largest resources of Kangzang and consolidate the Southwest border defense, which will greatly benefit our country's politics, military affairs, and economy. That is the eighth advantage. Now the Longhai Railway has reached Xi'an, and the Tongpu Railway is also about to be realized. If the Qinyu Railway is connected to Chengdu-Chongqing, it can promote the connection between Chengdu and Xi'an and link with the Longhai Road. In the future, it can directly start from Haizhou, the most advantageous port on the west coast of the Pacific Ocean, and connect with the British Indian Railway, forming the largest trunk line running across the interior of the country. Furthermore, in the future, by connecting with the Tongpu Line, it can also run through the Chahar-Suiyuan Special Region and the provinces of Shanxi, Gansu, Sichuan, Guizhou, Guangxi, and Guangdong, forming the largest trunk line running vertically through the interior of the country. This is not only in the development of southwestern transportation, but also in connecting the northeastern lifeline. That is the ninth advantage. Furthermore, when the British requested to lay the Shaxing-Guangchong lines in the second year of the Republic of China, the French had a petition to build this line. At that time, all the officials present believed that it should be actively built to avoid repeating the mistakes of Manchuria. Now Xiang is adopting public opinion, and everyone agrees. Furthermore, because it concerns the southwest, I dare to present it again in detail. Please investigate, verify, and forward it to the Lord for his wise judgment. If it is approved, please issue a clear order to specify the date for implementation so that Xiang can prepare according to the route through Sichuan, and the construction can be easily successful. The Southwest is fortunate, and Sichuan is fortunate. I am eagerly awaiting your instructions. Your brother, Liu Xiang, kowtows."

Ma Hongkui's Troops Move from Xu to Anhui

The First Division, led by Xu Tingyao, arrives in Xuzhou with the Division Headquarters.

The Third Division began entering Xuzhou City on the 10th to garrison.

Xuzhou Dispatch: There had been rumors for some time about the transfer of Ma Hongkui's 11th Army stationed in Xuzhou. Ma himself went to Beijing a few days ago to pay respects to Chiang and to inquire about his mother's illness. He returned to Xuzhou yesterday morning and immediately ordered his troops to pack up and move out. According to sources in the 11th Army, Ma Fuxiang has been appointed as the Chairman of Anhui Province, and Ma Hongkui has been appointed as the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in Anhui Province. Ma's entire force is moving to Anhui. Four trains on the Jinpu Railway are being used for round-trip transportation. The infantry will first take the train to Linhuai Pass and then transfer to Anqing. The cavalry will travel overland to Shouzhou. This morning (the 10th), the 1st Regiment (Lu Zhongliang), the 2nd Regiment (Li Decang), and the mortar battalion (Che Youde) of Ma Quanliang's 1st Brigade of the 64th Division have already departed south on three trains. The 3rd Regiment (Ma Yizhong), the training regiment (Li Yuying), the engineering battalion (Wang Xiangsheng), and the artillery battalion (Jin Zhongren) will follow. The 4th, 5th, and 6th Regiments of Ma Baolin's 2nd Brigade will be dispatched after the first batch of transport trains returns to Xuzhou. Ma Hongkui will wait until his troops have finished departing before leading the army headquarters and the special service regiment (Wang Tingru) to the south. Today, the various units are boarding trains at the Jiulishan Barracks, and the transport is very busy. It will probably take three or four days to complete the transport. Starting today, the city defense of Xuzhou will be handed over by the 64th Division and taken over by the 3rd Division.

The 2nd Brigade (Tang Junde) of the First Division has arrived in Xuzhou. The 1st Brigade (Hu Zongnan) is continuing to depart from Pukou. This morning, Xu Tingyao, the deputy commander of the First Division, and Liu Defang, the chief of staff of the Division Headquarters, also led personnel from the Division Headquarters and the special service battalion on a special train to Xuzhou, setting up the Division Headquarters at the Zhejiang Guild Hall's art school. Personnel from the staff, adjutant, quartermaster, military law, and medical departments have arrived in Xuzhou one after another. The directly subordinate artillery battalion (Chen Xiaojiang) has also arrived south of Xuzhou. Other units are arriving in succession. According to Xu, when interviewed at the station, Liu Zhi, the Commander-in-Chief, will not arrive in Xuzhou for several days. In addition to the headquarters moving to Xuzhou, the newly formed 23rd Division (Li Yunjie), the Independent 12th Brigade (Peng Jinliu), the Independent 14th Brigade (Peng Qibiao), and the 1st Cavalry Brigade (An Juncai) will also be transferred to Xuzhou for garrison.

Chen Jicheng arrived in Xuzhou and set up the Division Headquarters at the old site of the Wu Clan Elementary School in the South Gate. His troops have also all arrived. Since the 11th Army has moved south, Chen's Division Headquarters has moved to the old Daoyin Office in the city to take over city defense. His 8th Brigade (Li Yutang) has moved west to Huangkou to take over the defense left by the 11th Army. Part of the 9th Brigade is still defending south of Xuzhou. (10th)

He Chengjun Arrives in Hankou

The Provincial Government will be established after the National Government's official order arrives in Hubei.

The Wuhan Garrison will be temporarily represented by He.

Hankou Dispatch: He Chengjun previously went to Beijing from Hankou to report to Chairman Chiang on the military operations against Tang Shengzhi and to request to resign from his concurrent position as Chairman of the Hubei Provincial Government. Chiang personally comforted him and persuaded him to stay. The Hubei Provincial Government happened to be reorganized by a resolution of the Central Political Conference, with He still serving as the chairman. After completing his mission in Beijing, He took the Jiangyu steamer west on the 7th with Wang Jinyu, the commander of the 9th Army. Because he went to Anhui to meet with Wu Xingya, the newly appointed Director of the Civil Affairs Department of Hubei, and stayed for a short time, he did not arrive in Hankou until 3:00 p.m. on the 10th. After landing, He, Wang Jinyu, Xu Yuanquan, and Chiang Ting-wen took a car to the office of the Provincial Government in Hankou for a rest. Important military and political figures rushed to the office and had a long talk with He. I also visited shortly afterward. He's comments were as follows: (A) Regarding provincial affairs: (I asked) The central government has recently announced the members of the Hubei Provincial Government. Please introduce their brief histories. (He replied) I was not consulted in advance about the members appointed by the central government, but the central government was very cautious in its selection. For example, Wu Xingya, the Director of the Civil Affairs Department, has followed the Premier for many years, then followed Chairman Chiang, and has made many achievements. He is currently the Director of the Civil Affairs Department of Anhui Province and has served as acting chairman several times, with outstanding political reputation. Zhang Guanshi, the Director of the Finance Department, assisted Chiang in everything when he ran the Whampoa Military Academy. During the Northern Expedition, he served in various military supply positions. Huang Jianzhong, the Director of the Education Department, is currently the Director of the Education Department and has been involved in education for many years with Cai Yuanpei and Chiang Menglin. The only ones who came to Hubei with me this time are General Wang Jinyu and various staff members. (Asked) When will the new provincial government be established? (Answered) The National Government has not yet formally issued the order to reorganize the Hubei Provincial Government. I have ordered Chief Secretary Hua to telegraph Beijing to urge its early promulgation so that there is a basis for establishing the new provincial government as soon as possible. Before the National Government's order arrives in Hubei, I have ordered the directors of the various departments to hand over their affairs first to avoid interruption. (Asked) It is rumored that Peng Jieshi has been appointed as the Chief Secretary of the Provincial Government. Is this true? (Answered) It has not yet been decided. (Asked) Mr. He, will you return to Hubei this time to focus on provincial affairs, or to focus on military affairs, or to take care of both? (Answered) I have never been familiar with politics and have firmly declined several times to the central government, but my request was not granted, so I have no choice but to work hard. Fortunately, the military situation is now stable, so I can take care of both provincial government and military affairs. (Asked) Will the entire province's pacification affairs be handled by the provincial government? How will the troops be distributed? (Answered) The pacification of Hubei was previously handled by the Second Route Headquarters. Now that the Second Route has been transferred to the Jinpu Line, it will be the responsibility of the Wuhan Headquarters. As for how the pacification troops will be distributed, I have consulted with the Commander-in-Chief in Beijing and have made a general decision. It is also planned to complete the pacification work in three months. (Asked) It is rumored that Xu Yuanquan will be appointed as the Commander of the Provincial Garrison. Is this true? (Answered) Xu Yuanquan is currently serving as the Garrison Commander of the southern section of the Pinghan Line. The rumor about the Commander of the Provincial Garrison is not true. When I was in Beijing, because the candidate for the Wuhan Garrison Commander was not yet determined, I asked the Commander-in-Chief for instructions. I was informed that Director Liu had canceled this title when he took over the Wuhan Garrison. The Executive Yuan also has a resolution that no garrison commanders should be established in the provinces. Currently, only Beiping retains this title. (B) Regarding military affairs: (Asked) Will the troops of the Fifth Route Army be transferred to Hubei recently? (Answered) The 47th Division (Wang Jinyu) has been transferred to Xiangyang. General Wang has resigned from his position as Chairman of Anhui Province during this trip to Beijing. The 48th Division (Xu Yuanquan) and the New 4th Division (Liu Guitang) have been transferred to garrison the southern section of the Pinghan Line. The 54th Division (Wei Yisan) and the 14th Division (Liu Chunrong) have been transferred to garrison near Wusheng Pass. (Asked) Before Director He comes to Hankou, Commander-in-Chief Chiang Ting-wen is temporarily acting as the head of the Wuhan Headquarters. Chiang's Second Army and Ninth Division have heavy responsibilities, and his old illness has relapsed. He has repeatedly telegraphed Beijing to firmly decline. It is rumored that Mr. He will take over. Is this true? (Answered) Director He is still in charge of the Wuhan Headquarters. General Chiang is only acting as the head. Now that he has firmly declined, I will be responsible in the future. It will only be a short-term agency. (Asked) Who will command Yue Weijun's and Li Yunlong's troops in the future? (Answered) All troops in Hubei are under the command of the Wuhan Headquarters. At this point, I excused myself. It is reported that Mr. He will go to the Provincial Government on the morning of the 11th to inspect and convene a first conversation meeting with the members in Hubei to discuss the organization of the provincial government. (February 10)

Li Liejun Fights Fiercely with Bandits in His Hometown

Liu Zhi Sends Independent 16th Brigade to Aid from Yangxin

Nanchang Dispatch: Li Liejun returned to Jiangxi from Beijing last year and has been reading and writing in his hometown, Wuning County, and co-authoring the History of the Great War of the Republic of China with his Japanese friend Inoue. However, Wuning is located in northern Jiangxi, between Ruichang and Xiushui, and is connected to Yangxin and Tongshan in southern Hubei. The mountains are dense, and transportation is obstructed, making it an area where bandits and communists frequently appear. In January of last year, dozens of shops in Li Xi, in that county, were burned down by bandits, leaving not a single tile remaining. As a result, there were rumors that Li had been kidnapped by bandits. Those who had known Li inquired about it, but in fact, Li was safe and sound. In May of last year, Li moved to Mount Lu to live until the autumn when the weather on Mount Lu became too cold, and he returned to Wuning to handle local autonomy and continue to build the Wuning-Automobile Road (from Wuning to the Jiabu Station of the Nanshan Railway, which is two-thirds completed). Recently, due to the relatively small number of troops stationed in northern Jiangxi, bandits and communists have been rampant. At the beginning of this month, a large group of local bandits, more than a thousand, from the border between Jiangxi and Hubei attacked Wuning very fiercely. Li, who had been a soldier for a long time, remained calm and ordered the captain of the county's Security Brigade to quickly supervise the team to suppress the bandits. At the same time, he personally led his pistol and mobile machine gun guards to supervise the battle, which greatly boosted morale. The fighting was very fierce. The Captain of the Security Brigade, unfortunately, was shot and killed. Li continued to advance and finally repelled the bandits. According to sources in political circles, Li is deeply afraid that the bandits will come again and has telegraphed Liu Zhi, the Commander-in-Chief in Hankou, and Chairman Lu and Division Commander Zhang in Nanchang, requesting them to send troops to suppress the bandits immediately. It is reported that Liu, after receiving the telegram, has telegraphed Deng Ying's Independent 16th Brigade, stationed in Yangxin and Tongcheng, to immediately go to Wuning to suppress the bandits and communists in that county and Tonggu. At the same time, the province has dispatched a small motorboat from Wucheng up the Xiushui River to Wucheng to welcome Li to the province or Jiujiang for a temporary stay to avoid danger and ensure his safety. (8th)

Local Dispatch

Songjiang

Another Country Gentleman Weakens: Mr. Lei Putong, a country gentleman, started his career from an outstanding background. His morality and literary works were greatly admired. He served in Beijing for twenty years, transferred from the Ministry of Agriculture to the Translation Office, and promoted from a ministerial official to a senior counselor. In the Guangxu Dingwei year, he was specially appointed as the Minister to Austria. His negotiations and diplomatic skills were admired at home and abroad. After completing his term, he returned to China and retired to his hometown, residing in the South Dike, refusing to go out. He then called himself Wei Yin. Later, when Song County was preparing to revise the local gazetteer, Mr. Lei was invited to be the editor-in-chief. Last summer, due to editing the gazetteer too much, his right arm became very painful. Medical treatment was ineffective, and he passed away on the 30th day of the 11th month of the lunar calendar. The people of Songjiang all respected and mourned him. It is now reported that a memorial service will be held on the 27th of this month in the Gregorian calendar. It is expected that the plain carriages and white horses will be a grand occasion at that time.

Suzhou

Key Criminals in the Wuzhen Robbery Captured in Suzhou: The City Public Security Bureau, led by District Chief Min and Inspector Ding Lei, captured two bandits at No. 20 Xidajie, Panmen, the day before yesterday (the 11th). It is reported that the captured bandits, Cao Wen (also known as Cao Er Shaoye) and Fu Chun, were related to the lake bandits and were the key criminals who robbed Wuzhen, Zhejiang on December 27 of last year. The Chief of the City Public Security Bureau has telegraphed the Zhejiang Provincial Civil Affairs Department to send personnel to Suzhou to escort them back for handling.

Wujin County Court Established: The Jiangsu Higher Court has made preparations for the Wujin County Court. President Lin specially ordered Wu Zengshan, the president of the court, to establish the court on the 16th of this month and take over all case files and documents from the former judicial section. The Nantong County Court is also scheduled to be established within this month.

Reward Offered for the Capture of Taihu Bandit Leaders: Gong, the District Chief of the Third Water Public Security District, attended the Bandit Suppression Conference of the Shanghai Garrison Headquarters the day before yesterday and has now returned to Suzhou. It is said that after the establishment of the Bandit Suppression Headquarters, General Commander Hu's plan will be divided into: 1) Offering a high reward for the capture of bandit leaders; 2) Launching a unified team to suppress the lake bandits; 3) Handing over the captured bandits to the General Headquarters for disposal according to law, with important ones being executed on the spot.

Qingpu

Robberies Occur in Succession: Chen Jinghua, a farmer from Guanwangmiao Village in the fourth district of Qingpu, Xie Bosun and Xie Zhongxian, residents of Mitian Village, and Lu Pingyu, a farmer from a certain village, were all suddenly attacked by more than a dozen bandits around 8 pm the day before yesterday, who broke in and suffered incalculable losses. Yao Renbai and his grandson, residents of Fangjia Yao Town, were also kidnapped by bandits the day before yesterday. It is reported that they have all submitted petitions to the county government for arrest and rescue.

Xia Xiaolin Loves Gambling More Than Life: Xia Xiaolin, from a certain town in Qingpu, is in his thirties, has a wife and a son, and works in a fruit store in the town. He is addicted to gambling and opium. The day before yesterday, he lost all his savings at a gambling den. Xia wanted to make a comeback, so he pawned the cotton quilt, clothes, and his wife's jewelry, getting more than twenty yuan, and went to the gambling den again. The result was still a defeat, and he was at a loss. He had the thought of ending his life, so he swallowed a large amount of opium the night before yesterday, intending to commit suicide. He slept until midnight when the poison took effect, and he rolled around in bed. His wife was very alarmed and immediately called a doctor for treatment. Fortunately, Xia was addicted to opium, and it did not cost him his life.

Wuxi

First District Requests to Implement Feast Donation: The Wuxi feast donation case was previously drafted into regulations by the Education Bureau, submitted to the Provincial Department and County for approval, and decided to begin implementation in February of this year. It is currently being actively pursued. Recently, the township and deputy chiefs of the First District (Wuxi City), considering that the autonomous expenses have not yet been settled, resolved at the district affairs meeting on the 8th of this month to implement the feast autonomous donation based on the provisions of Article 11, Paragraph 5 of Chapter 6 of the Township Autonomy Implementation Law, specifically to fund district and township autonomy. Mu Suchen and Fang Mengqi were specifically designated to petition the County Government, personally presenting the request. County Magistrate Sun agreed to forward it for approval. The district office has also drafted a brief charter for the donation, requesting the county to forward it to the provincial department.

Meningitis Spreads Terrifyingly: The Wuxi Municipal Preparation Office received an urgent telegram from the Civil Affairs Department yesterday, stating that in the past ten days, there have been outbreaks of epidemic cerebrospinal meningitis in the provincial capital and Baoshan County, resulting in a large number of deaths. It ordered a prompt investigation to determine whether there have been any cases of this epidemic within its jurisdiction and to take appropriate precautions to prevent its spread. After receiving the order, the office found that there have also been cases of this epidemic within the city. Hospitals have reported approximately sixty to seventy patients in total, with more than ten deaths, mostly children. In addition to reporting to the Civil Affairs Department, the Social Affairs Section also proposed at the 29th office meeting to discuss preventive measures.

District Chiefs Complete Internship: The county's district intern chiefs had their internship results reviewed by County Magistrate Sun at the end of the year and reported to the Civil Affairs Department for formal appointment. The instructions have now been received, along with sixteen appointment letters, which have been forwarded to the respective district chiefs for acknowledgement. The county has a total of seventeen districts. Except for Yuan Shikui, the district chief of the fifteenth district, who remains in internship due to an ongoing case, Su Weibin, the district chief of the sixth district, has also been instructed to exercise caution due to his impetuous handling of affairs.

Changzhou

More Communists Captured: The Second Squad of the Wuyi Police, at around 9 PM on the 10th, captured two Danyang communists, Yang Jinxiu and Jiang Shurong, along with seven patrons, including Lu Jin, at the residence of a prostitute, Xie Fengying, at the end of Gongjia Lane. They were all taken to the squad along with Xie Fengying. After interrogation, Lu Jin and the other seven patrons, as well as Xie Fengying, were found to be uninvolved and were released on bail. Yang Jinxiu confessed that there were two other accomplices, Shi Sanling and A San, carrying firearms, hiding in Zhao Ji Bao's restaurant under the Diaqiao Bridge outside Xiaonanmen. At around 6 AM on the 11th, a squad was dispatched to Zhao's house for a search, and the harboring Zhao Ji Bao and four communist fugitives, Li Jinwen, He Genpei, A San, and Shi Sanling, were captured on the spot. After interrogation, they confessed that two guns were hidden in the house of Lu Qisheng in Dongzhuang Village, Dezexiang, outside Dabeimen. The police captain immediately sent Detective Fang to lead a squad to Dongzhuang Village for a search. Lu Qisheng had already fled upon hearing the news. A suitcase was found in his mistress Xu Shi's house, containing two box guns and multiple bullets. Xu Shi and He Xu were then taken to the squad for interrogation. The witnesses were transferred to the brigade headquarters by Captain Chen for further investigation by the county on the 12th.

Preventing Communist Activities: Li Leng, the Director of the Wuyi Public Security Bureau, learned that there were rumors of communist activities in Qishuyan. He specifically instructed Captain Mu Ke to send a detective chief to lead a squad of squad leaders to temporarily reside at the town's Public Security Branch to provide security.

Changshu

Provincial Approval of Rice Guild Dispute: Regarding the case of a dispute between Lu Rusheng and Lu Gongquan of the local rice industry guild during a meeting convened last month on the 8th to discuss reorganization, which led to litigation, Lu Rusheng and others submitted a public petition to the Construction Department, requesting the county to severely punish the matter. The Construction Department issued an instruction stating that the rice industry sub-association has no authority to take over the guild, and the rice industry labor union should still be reorganized according to the law. Lu Gongquan's irregular actions have been ordered to be investigated by the county and severely punished according to the law, and the county public security bureau's one-sided detention has been reprimanded on file. It is hereby notified.

Personnel Registration Forms Arrive in Changshu: Wu Xinheng, the District Chief of the First District, was commissioned by the county magistrate last week to go to the Provincial Department to collect the personnel registration forms. Wu has returned to Changshu after completing his mission on the 10th of this month.

Nantong

Fierce Battle Between Police and Bandits at Wujie Bridge: A large group of bandits suddenly appeared at the border of Nantong and Rugao counties, engaging in rampant arson and looting. The police and militia rushed to Wujie Bridge to intercept them, resulting in a fierce battle lasting four hours. More than ten hardened bandits were killed in action, five were captured, and more than ten rifles and two earth cannons were seized. The police suffered three casualties. The bandit leader was killed in action, and his head was hung in Pingchao Market as a warning. On the 11th, County Magistrate Chen led a machine gun squad to the Siyu Port area to suppress the bandits.

Requesting Early Establishment of County Court by Telegram: The Nantong County Court has been completed. The Nantong, Chongming, Haimen, and Taixing General Chamber of Commerce and other organizations have sent a telegram to the High Court requesting the early establishment of the County Court to comply with the rule of law.

Verdict in Case of American Automobile Accident: An American, Schmidt, was driving a car on Chengzha Road and struck and killed boatman Xie Miaobao. After trial by the criminal court of the County Government, Schmidt was sentenced to a fine of one hundred yuan for negligence. In the private prosecution, Schmidt reached a settlement with the family of the deceased, providing compensation and closing the case.

General Chamber of Commerce Prepares for Reorganization: The Nantong, Chongming, Haimen, and Taixing General Chamber of Commerce has been ordered by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to reorganize. A reorganization committee has been established to handle the process.

Jiangyin

Investigating Murder for Money Case: A murder for money case occurred at Tangjia Bridge, Shiqi Tenth Section. Yesterday (the 11th) afternoon, Judge Tong Cheng held a court session to question the suspects. Wu Xirong testified, stating, "I am fifty-four years old and live at Tangjia Bridge. Axi is from the courtyard, and his son is called Bingquan. He is from his uncle's family, so his surname is Wang. I have no animosity with Wu Rukang, and there is no feud over grain transport. He said I murdered him, which is a false accusation. I was already in bed and didn't know anything about it." The judge asked, "Then how was the bloody clothing found in your house?" He replied, "I don't know. I don't want to leave either. I don't know where my son went. I don't know when he came back that night. I ate with my son that night, and he went to Qingyang to get yarn and then went to sleep. I don't know where the bloody clothing came from. The deceased is completely wronging me," and so on. Wu Axi testified, "I am fifty-nine years old and live at Tangjia Bridge. I watch the hermitage at Yueyu Terrace. I ate dinner at the hermitage on the evening of the ninth with a total of seven tables. Rukang handled the money. The Buddhist association has been going on for two years and is now complete for the year. There are more than fifty people attending the Buddhist association. After dinner, I stayed inside. I didn't see Wu Xirong, Xia Aliou, etc. Later, around 5 o'clock, I saw Wang Bingjin and Xia Aliou at the riverbank from above the latrine. I went inside. I was arrested by the security corps the next day." The judge asked, "Did you change your clothes?" Axi replied, "I didn't change. The village chief is against me and is biting me. I have a disagreement with my daughter-in-law and went out to watch the hermitage." The judge ordered the removal of his mandarin jacket, lined robe, and long gown for inspection, and there were no bloodstains. Axi testified, "The village chief is a bao head and has a grudge against me. Rukang also has a grudge because of being a director. When I saw people at the riverbank, dinner hadn't been served yet. Rukang went back after eating dinner. Rukang insisted that I was slandering him because I was on good terms with the village chief," and so on. After the interrogation, they were detained, awaiting the arrest and interrogation of Wu Bingquan and Xia Aliou. Yesterday (the 11th), the family of the deceased held a large memorial service and went to Wu Xirong's house to make a scene, taking away three cows and three pigs, having already slaughtered one, and destroying all the farming tools and other items. Xirong's wife, Huang, went to the county government yesterday to file a complaint.

Investigating Prison Break of Inmates: On the 31st of last month, three inmates, anti-revolutionaries Zhu Asan and Zhu Asi, and thief Zhang Abao, escaped from prison. The guard Sun Lie was arrested. In the afternoon of the 11th, Judge Tong Cheng questioned Sun Tongnian and Yang Lianzi, who were in the same cell. According to Sun Lie's testimony, "I am sixty years old and live at the entrance of Yimiao Lane. I have been a guard for more than ten years without interruption. I was very careful when I went on duty on the 31st. It happened very quickly. Warden Liu didn't collect the seal. I asked to collect the seal, but he said it didn't matter. I was guarding eighty-one people alone without anyone else. I didn't know anything about the digging of the hole. There was no hint of it. The warden didn't collect the seal, saying it was a New Year's custom. I had no bribery or connivance. Please investigate." Sun Tongnian testified, "I am in the same cell with Shen Lingen, Ren Ashi, Zhu Asi, etc. I didn't hear anything when the incident happened. Zhu Asan and Zhu Asi didn't sleep together with me at night." Yang Lianzi testified, "I was sentenced to two years for trafficking in illicit salt. Zhu Asi dug the hole. I was already asleep. That day, the prison official said he wouldn't collect the seal, saying it was a rare day all year round. It wasn't us who asked not to collect the seal," and then he said loudly, "The prison officials deduct our rations. Although we are supposed to get 1 jiao and 1 fen per day, we only get 15 liang of rice at most. They deduct 3 liang from us. We demand adjustment." The judge ordered them to be remanded and told them to behave themselves before adjourning.

Zhenjiang

Construction Department Allocates Funds for Dam Construction: The Jiangbei Canal Engineering Office previously submitted a report to the Construction Department requesting the allocation of funds to first build the south side of Huoyao Sluice and the east and west dams of Xiwang River, estimating a total cost of over three thousand silver dollars. After review by the Construction Department, the estimated cost was deemed appropriate, and it was approved to first allocate one thousand five hundred yuan, with the remainder to be allocated subsequently.

County Magistrate Zhang Scheduled to Take Oath: Zhang Peng, the Acting Magistrate of Zhenjiang County, took office on the 25th of last month after receiving his seal. It was decided at a provincial government meeting yesterday to change "Acting" to "Acting on Behalf." The swearing-in ceremony is scheduled to be held at 10 AM on the 18th of this month.

Chamber of Commerce Retains Three Standing Committee Members: Lu Xiaobo, Hu Jianchun, and Zhang Yongshao, the Standing Committee Members of the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce, previously requested to resign due to busy schedules. The executive and supervisory committees of the Chamber of Commerce resolved to unanimously retain them yesterday.

Jiaxing

Large Number of Refugees Arrive at Shuangqiao: More than a thousand refugees suddenly arrived at Shuangqiao Town, about eight or nine li outside the North Gate of Jiaxing, at around 6 PM the other day. They arrived on one hundred and thirty-six boats. These refugees were all from Funing, Jiangsu. After the boats docked, the refugees disembarked one after another. The residents of the town were greatly alarmed. The police chief of the stationed Public Security Branch, along with the police, persuaded and stopped the refugees from disembarking while reporting to the Third Public Security Bureau. Director Chen telegraphed the County Public Security Bureau to dispatch a police detachment to the town for suppression. The next morning, village chief Wu Xiaoting handed over 55 yuan to Yang Xushu, the general representative of the refugees, as food rations and urged them to leave the area. The refugees then boarded their original boats and headed towards Wangjiangjing and Songjiang.

Tian Qingting Files Another Appeal: Jiaxing Jianqiao Elementary School had 1,000 yuan stolen from its savings account in August of last year. Including the lost cash, the total was 1,119 yuan. Tian Qingting, a former teacher at the school, was considered a prime suspect. The court summoned Tian for questioning and sentenced him to one year and two months in prison and ordered him to repay the money. Tian appealed the verdict, and the Hangzhou County Local Branch Court summoned witnesses and held a hearing. The appeal was rejected, and the original verdict was upheld. It is now known that Tian has filed another appeal with the High Court.

Jiashan

Reasons for Dismissal of Prison Official: Wang, the prison official of Jiashan County Government, was usually negligent in his duties. On the 6th of last month, Warden Xu, along with inmate Sun Laosi, was escorting foreign socks to the Huihe Sock Factory at the worksite. They privately released the inmate, who did not return for ten days. When the official became anxious and searched for him, the inmate's whereabouts were unknown. It was difficult to conceal the matter, so he reported it to County Magistrate Wu, who ordered a thorough search. The inmate was found in Shanghai and escorted back to Jiashan. After interrogation by the County Court, the inmate confessed that Warden Xu had allowed him to go out to borrow money and find a way to make a living in Shanghai. When Xu was questioned, his answers were evasive, and he was immediately dismissed from his post and ordered to await further legal action. The superiors, considering that Prison Warden Wang had failed to manage the prison effectively, ordered his dismissal and transfer to the provincial capital, and Xiao was appointed to fill the vacancy, scheduled to take over on the 15th.

Refugee Disturbance Suppressed and Deported: More than a hundred refugees from Huai and Si were causing disturbances in the northern part of the county, stealing chickens, seizing ducks, picking up rice, and taking firewood. Yesterday, they lingered and caused trouble in the Lujia River area. Village farmers urgently reported to the Xitang Public Security Branch, who went to suppress them and deport them.

Ningbo

Trial of Rioters in Liuheng: The residents of Liuheng Island in Dinghai gathered in a riot. Commander Wang sent a warship together with the County Magistrate of Dinghai, leading more than four hundred soldiers and police to suppress the riot and capture ninety rioters, who were taken to the county for detention. It is now known that Wu Chun, the County Magistrate of Dinghai, brought many official documents to the province yesterday to report the details. He also sent his secretary, He Runzhang, to act as his deputy and invited representatives from various public organizations and the party to interrogate the rioters from Liuheng Island, starting at 8 AM on the 9th. The interrogation continued until 7 PM. It resumed at 7 AM the next morning and concluded at 12 PM. During the interrogation, more than ten people, including Hu Dabing and Zhang Ashui, confessed without hesitation, saying that Wang Gengkui and others were indeed local bullies in Liuheng and that killing them would eliminate harm. After the interrogation, more than seventy people were shackled. However, the shackles previously owned by the Dinghai County Office were insufficient, so Tie Zuo was asked to rush to make three pairs of shackles each, which is truly a major prison case that has never happened before.

Kidnapping and Assault Case in Yaobei: Chen Xianlu of Gaowang Town, Yaobei, runs a wine and rice shop at home and has considerable savings. His eldest son, Chen Anji, is currently a clerk at the Jiangsu Shatien Official Property Bureau of the Ministry of Finance. He returned home on the 5th to visit his relatives. On the evening of the 6th, six bandits suddenly entered the shop and grabbed the shop owner Chen Xianlu and his youngest son Chen Bingji, demanding 500 yuan. Bingji pretended to go inside to get the money and took the opportunity to escape. The bandits, waiting for the youngest son to come out, kidnapped the old miser Chen Xianlu and fired a shot into the air as a warning. Chen's son, Anji, happened to be at a dinner party at a neighbor's house. Hearing the sound of gunfire at home, he hurried home. Just as he reached the front door, the bandits fired a shot, and the bullet pierced his left flank. He was still able to swim across the river to escape. The bandits then kidnapped Chen Xianlu and fled south. After his eldest son, Anji, escaped by swimming, neighbors carried him home, where he was unconscious. Yesterday, his family invited a doctor to diagnose him, who said that his lung corner was injured. If his fever does not increase, he may be saved.

Important Education News

Education Program Meeting

First Day Passes Elementary Program

The Education Program Drafting Committee of the Ministry of Education held a meeting at the Ministry of Education at 3 PM on the 11th. Those present were Tao Xingzhi, Tao Xuan, Dai Xiujun, Yu Ziyi, Zhao Naichuan, Jiang Shaomo, Liu Dabai, Huang Jianzhong, Yu Wencan, Zhu Jingnong, Chen Jianshu, Yang Fang, Chu Minyi, Gao Weichang, etc. Chu Minyi chaired the meeting, and Gao Weichang took minutes. The discussion on the elementary education program was extensive and quite interesting. By 5:30 PM, the elementary program had been revised and passed. The committee then solicited opinions from each member for one week. After one week, the original drafters will reorganize it, which will be regarded as the final plan. Due to the lateness of the hour, it was decided to continue the meeting at 9 AM on the 12th to discuss the normal school, secondary, and higher education programs. It is hoped that the strength of the day will be used to completely discuss these two programs.

He Yingqin Requests Allocation of Funds for Students Studying in France and Germany

Totaling 116,800+ Yuan

Executive Yuan Has Approved Order for Military to Allocate Funds

He Yingqin, the Director-General of Training, was previously ordered to handle the examination of the sixth graduating class of the Central Military Academy for studying military affairs in Europe and the United States to deepen their studies. Twenty-one regular students and nineteen alternate students were admitted. The regular students were sent to England and the United States in advance, and the alternate students were sent to France and Germany later. He immediately wrote to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to investigate military enrollment in Europe and the United States and the required expenses, and prepared a budget for dispatch. The budget for studying in England and the United States, 176,660 yuan, has been ordered by the Ministry of Military Administration to be allocated by the Military Supplies Department. Now, the second batch of students studying in France and Germany is also about to depart. He specifically prepared a budget of 116,840 yuan a few days ago and submitted it to Chairman Jiang of the National Government for review and order to be allocated by the military supplies department so that they can be dispatched in due course. After the National Government received the report, a civil servant wrote to the Executive Yuan to forward the matter for handling. Yesterday, the Executive Yuan ordered the Ministry of Military Administration to instruct the Military Supplies Department to allocate the funds.

Ministry of Education Pays Attention to Sending Government-Funded Students

Must Strictly Test Language of Study Abroad Country

The Ministry of Education recently issued an order to the education administrative agencies of various provinces and cities, stating, "It has been found that students studying in various countries often spend time learning the language of the study abroad country after arriving, which is a pity. In the future, no matter what examination method is used to dispatch government-funded students, the language of the study abroad country must be strictly tested to ensure that reading, writing, conversation, and listening comprehension are all unimpeded. This will avoid wasting time on tutoring and wasting public funds. In addition to separate orders, the relevant departments must comply with this order."

Eighth General Meeting

(1) Shandong Provincial Secondary School Training Standards and Implementation Methods. Resolution: (A) The title is revised to "Shandong Provincial Secondary School Provisional Training Standards and Implementation Methods." (B) The item "The Meaning of Training" is submitted to the nominated committee for revision with reference to the following opinions. In the meaning of training, add a specific opinion under "leading them on the right track" as follows: (1) Cultivate talents who can build a Three Principles of the People society. (2) Suit the Three Principles of the People society. (3) Create a backbone to realize the Three Principles of the People. (4) Actively develop their vitality to create sound members of the Three Principles of the People. (5) Create sound citizens and realize the Three Principles of the People. (6) The word "meaning" in the meaning of training is submitted to the committee for revision. (C) In the item "Standards of Training," (1) Ideology: According to the review opinion, revise to "Understand the Three Principles of the People, Believe in the Three Principles of the People, and Practice the Three Principles of the People." (2) Revolutionization: According to the review opinion, revise to "Determine a revolutionary outlook on life and cultivate revolutionary talents." (3) Populism: Original proposal. (4) Socialization: Revise "promote culture" by deleting the four words, and add the word "discipline" to the clause, which is submitted to the committee for revision. (5) Scientification: The words "cultivate" and "volunteer" in the original clause are submitted to the committee for revision. (6) Artification: The clause is submitted to the committee for re-drafting. It is already 12 o'clock at this point. This case has not yet been fully discussed. The ninth general meeting will continue the discussion this afternoon. Chairman Peng Baichuan made a temporary motion to extend the meeting by five minutes to report on the points to be noted when preparing the budget for each school in the 19th year: (1) The cost of meals for normal school students is calculated at 40 students per class, 5 yuan per person per month, 10 months per year, and listed as a separate independent budget. (2) The First Rural Normal School adds two classes. The school will set up a central elementary school calculated with five classes. (3) The Second and Third Rural Normal Schools are calculated with two classes each. The central elementary school will be established later. (4) The Fourth Middle School adds one senior high school class. (5) The Fifth Middle School adds one junior high school class and one senior high school class. (6) The Eighth Middle School adds one junior high school class and one commercial high school class. (7) The Seventh Middle School adds one junior high school class. (8) The Sixth Middle School reduces one junior high school class and adds one senior high school class. (9) The First Women's Middle School adds two junior high school classes. (10) The Twelfth Middle School adds two junior high school classes. (11) The experimental fees for the seven vocational schools total 35,000 yuan. (12) The standard for teaching salaries in secondary schools is calculated at 36 hours per week. (13) The office expenses of secondary schools outside the province may be increased as appropriate due to special circumstances, but the total increase for each school is limited to 5,000 yuan. (14) The cost of free tuition for poor students totals 10,000 yuan. (15) The experimental fee for each experimental elementary school is 5 yuan per class per month. (16) For each experimental elementary school with eight or more classes, add staff with a total salary of 30 yuan per month. (17) Each normal school elementary school is treated the same as an experimental elementary school. The meeting adjourned after the report was completed.

Party and Education Authorities Host Farewell Dinner for Party Members Studying Abroad

The Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters and the Shanghai Special City Education Bureau hosted a farewell banquet at the East Asia Restaurant yesterday for Party members, revolutionary youth dispatched by the Central Government to study abroad. Attendees included Pan Gongzhan, Tao Baichuan, Wu Bokang, Zhu Yingpeng, Tang Demin, Hou Dachun and other members of the Executive and Supervisory Committees of the Municipal Party Headquarters; Chen Dezheng, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau, Secretary Zheng Hechun, heads of various departments, all superintendents; and Party members studying abroad, Cao Liying, Zhao Shu and other guests, totaling more than 50 people. The seating began at 12:00 PM. Halfway through the dinner, Chairman Chen Dezheng rose to give a farewell speech, stating that the Party's dispatch of Party members to study abroad this time truly set a new record in the Party's history. Therefore, the mission undertaken by these comrades studying abroad is different from that of ordinary students studying abroad. Like ordinary students studying abroad, all of you have received higher education, but because you have participated in actual revolutionary movements, you understand both the special circumstances of China and the adaptation of the Party's revolutionary movement to China's special circumstances. All of you have returned from the front lines of the revolution to the reserves to cultivate your spirit and prepare your intellect. The future development of the Party in all aspects and the realization of the Three Principles of the People will depend on your efforts. You should understand that in the current period, the Party governs politics, politics serves education, education serves politics, and the Party establishes education. Your fundamental efforts will be even more helpful to the education that the Party values. In the past, the Party and education seemed to be separate, but in reality, the Party cannot be separated from education, nor can education be separated from the Party. The mission undertaken by those studying abroad is to promote education from the Party's standpoint and to clarify the Party's principles in the field of education. Therefore, both the Party and education have high hopes for the comrades studying abroad. Today, the Party and education are hosting a banquet for comrades studying abroad who are of great importance to both the Party and education. The significance of this is self-evident. Therefore, I hope that all comrades present will not forget this banquet and will not forget the different and special mission that Party members studying abroad undertake compared to ordinary students studying abroad.

Next, Pan Gongzhan gave a speech, the main points of which can be divided into three points: 1. Today, China urgently needs scientific talents. You must adopt their strengths and discard their weaknesses when studying abroad. 2. Current Party and government workers are like laborers engaged in the construction of the foundation. In the future, you will all be specialists, and the major affairs of the Party and the country will rely on your leadership. Therefore, you must cooperate with each other to achieve great things. 3. When you return to China after completing your studies, you will definitely benefit the Party and the country. You can continue to work hard as current Party and government workers. Subsequently, Wang Ke, a standing committee member of the Student Management Office, gave a speech. Cao Liying and Zou Degao, representatives of the students studying abroad, gave thank-you speeches. A group photo was taken to commemorate the occasion. The event ended in joy at 4:00 PM.

Vocational Guidance Center Introduces Specialists

The Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center has recently focused on vocational testing as an important task. This time, it has been entrusted by a silk factory to use testing methods to recruit three trainees as silk reeling factory management trainees. Applicants must be 18 to 22 years old, have a junior high school education or above, believe that they meet the qualifications, can endure hardship, and are interested in this industry. They can write to the center to request the articles of association and application form. Qualified applicants will be notified by the center for testing to determine acceptance. In addition, a vocational school nearby has commissioned the center to hire one rattan worker and one bamboo worker technician, each with a monthly salary of 20 yuan. A school in Guangxi has commissioned the center to hire one physical education teacher with a monthly salary of 60 yuan or more. The center has recently registered five professionals with overseas study experience: (1) Mr. Liu Yifu, Ph.D. in Philosophy from the University of Iowa, USA, has taught courses in Philosophy, Sociology, Education, English, and German at Guanghua University and Northeastern University; (2) Mr. Si Min, Master of Arts from Harvard University, USA, specializing in Philosophy, Logic, and English Literature; (3) Mr. Zhang Mingshou, Bachelor of Science in Electrical Engineering from Newcastle University, UK, has interned at Maowei Electric Factory in the UK for one or two years and at Luton Oil Engine Factory for a long time, capable of serving as a professor of power electronics and a power plant engineer; (4) Mr. Ma Zhichao, Master of Arts in Public Administration from New Jersey University, UK, Master of Business Administration from Northwestern University, USA, and Ph.D. from Jianxie City University, USA, has served as Director of the Foreign Exchange Department of the Zhicheng Savings Bank, Professor at New Jersey University, and Manager of Guangxi Industrial Bank; (5) Mr. Yang Mingzhen, graduated from the Department of Engineering, University of Chicago, USA, has worked in textile factories, specializing in textile engineering. Universities, factories, or administrative agencies that need to hire or discuss with the above talents can contact the center.

Local News

Yesterday's Discussion on Noble Methods for Relief Funds

Convened by the Office of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce

A Formal Meeting to Be Held Next Monday

A Recommendation to Be Submitted to the League of Nations

The Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce convened British and American magnates residing in Shanghai, as well as the Bankers Association, the Union of National Chambers of Commerce, the Bureau of Social Affairs, and other organizations at 3:30 PM yesterday to discuss methods for relieving the silver crisis. Chinese and foreign businessmen exchanged views, and at 5:00 PM, Western businessmen left early to attend the board meeting of the Engineering Bureau. The remaining representatives from various organizations discussed until 6:00 PM and decided to invite businessmen from France, Japan, Italy, and Germany to attend the formal discussion on Sino-foreign cooperation on relief methods next Monday (the 17th). The proceedings of yesterday's meeting are detailed on the left.

Attendees Yesterday's attendees included: On the Chinese side, Bei Songsun representing the Bankers Association, Hu Xisheng, Xu Jiyu, and Qin Runqing representing the Money Industry Association, Dong Keren and Section Chief Wu representing the Bureau of Social Affairs, Lin Kanghou representing the Union of National Chambers of Commerce, and Zhao Jinqing, Zhang Xianglin, Zhu Chengzhang, Shou Jingwei, and Xu Jianping. On the Western side, Lawson, General Manager of HSBC, Leimen, former President of the American Chamber of Commerce, Keer, General Manager of Xiangmao Foreign Firm and President of the British Chamber of Commerce, Xue Fo, General Manager of Jardine Matheson, and French, President of the American Chamber of Commerce, and more than ten others.

Opinions of Foreign Businessmen The meeting was first chaired by Zhao Jinqing, Director of the Office, who delivered a speech hoping that Chinese and foreign businessmen would cooperate thoroughly to relieve the decline in silver prices, and hoped that they would put forward various opinions as much as possible to serve as a reference for the government. Then, Xu Jianping, representing Kong Xiangxi, was introduced to give a welcome speech. Subsequently, various foreign businessmen expressed their opinions, which are summarized as follows: (1) To relieve the crisis, China itself should quickly restore transportation so that accumulated goods can be circulated at home and abroad. (2) Onerous taxes and miscellaneous levies should be abolished as soon as possible to develop domestic goods. (3) Half-dollar coins should be minted, and banks should have sufficient cash reserves when issuing banknotes.

Proposals Stipulated After the foreign businessmen left at 5:00 PM, representatives from various organizations continued to discuss. The opinions put forward by the representatives of the Bureau of Social Affairs were: (1) Prohibit the import of silver bullion; (2) Restrict the issuance of banknotes except by national banks; (3) Restrict trading on gold and silver exchanges. After discussion, it was agreed to first submit the next proposal so that opinions could be put forward at the next formal meeting. Zhao Jinqing then stipulated three proposals for the next formal meeting: (1) From the perspective of foreign businessmen, what policies should the Chinese government use to relieve the decline in silver prices, and what recommendations should China make at the exchange rate joint meeting of this year's League of Nations? (2) In what ways can Chinese and foreign businessmen in China work together to relieve the silver crisis?

Zhang Qun and Yang Shuzhuang Sailed to Fujian Yesterday

Mayor Zhang Qun has been preparing to set off since he was ordered to go to Fujian for investigation. Sino-Japanese Tariff Negotiations

Both Sides' Opinions Are Quite Close

Awaiting Instructions from the Japanese Government

According to the National News Agency, the Sino-Japanese tariff issue is one of the most important issues in the Sino-Japanese Commercial Treaty. Since repeated consultations between Chargé d'Affaires Shigemitsu and Ministers Song and Wang, a general compromise has been reached. The Japanese side has also agreed to and formally promised to resolve the preliminary issues raised by China. In recent days, they have been separately telegraphing each other about the types and rates of goods subject to reciprocal tariffs. On one hand, Consul Uemura in Beijing is negotiating with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Finance nearby, which has been quite satisfactory. The opinions of both sides are very close. Yesterday, Chargé d'Affaires Shigemitsu sent a special telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to report the details and request instructions. It is expected that a reply will be received in Shanghai within this week. Once approved, the date for signing the agreement will be determined, and negotiations on treaty revision will begin.

A Large Batch of Silver Coins Will Continue to Arrive from Saigon

Five Million Have Already Arrived in Shanghai

On the 3rd of this month, the Banque de l'Indochine shipped five million silver coins from Saigon. It is reported that a large batch of silver coins will continue to arrive in Shanghai. The bank initially planned to entrust the melting of the silver coins to various silver smelters. However, after repeated discussions on prices, no agreement was reached. Initially, the silver smelters set the price at 7 mace, 1 fen, 3 li, 2 hao, and a half. Later, after trial melting, they decided to abandon the deal because there was no profit to be made. It is now reported that the bank has entrusted the mint to conduct tests.

Ninety-Fourth Meeting

The Shanghai Special Municipality Executive Committee held its ninety-fourth standing committee meeting at 10:00 AM yesterday. Hua Shang Pudong Two Companies Sign Power Supply Contract

The Pudong Electric Company is not large in scale, and its power generation is not very economical, resulting in high electricity prices. Local people have expressed dissatisfaction. The company is following the Shanghai Public Utilities Bureau's plan to unify the city's power plants, and is negotiating with the Hua Shang Electric Company to supply power, in order to reduce costs and potentially lower electricity prices. Recently, the two companies agreed to lay a cross-river cable in the Dongjiadu area, stipulating that the project will be completed and power will be supplied within one year. The power supply contract has also been agreed upon by both parties and submitted to the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau for approval and filing.

Report of the Jianghai Customs 2.5% Surtax National Treasury Bond Fund Custody Committee

Situation from May 1927 to the End of 1929. The Jianghai Customs 2.5% Surtax National Treasury Bond Fund Custody Committee was established in May 1927. Up to the end of 1928, it had successively managed five types of treasury bond funds: (1) Jianghai Customs 2.5% Surtax National Treasury Bonds; (2) Reissued Jianghai Customs 2.5% Surtax National Treasury Bonds; (3) Tobacco Tax National Treasury Bonds; (4) Post-Rehabilitation Short-Term Public Bonds; (5) 1928 Financial Short-Term Public Bonds. A report was published at the end of 1928 for public viewing. In 1929, six types of public bonds and treasury bond funds were added to the management: (6) 1928 Financial Long-Term Public Bonds; (7) 1929 Disaster Relief Public Bonds; (8) 1929 Troop Reduction Public Bonds; (9) Reissued Tobacco Tax National Treasury Bonds; (10) 1929 Customs Duty Treasury Bonds; (11) 1929 Demobilization Treasury Bonds. The principal and interest of the various public bonds and treasury bonds managed by the Committee that have been repaid are as follows: (1) Jianghai Customs 2.5% Surtax National Treasury Bonds: Principal and interest have been paid in 30 installments and have been fully redeemed. (2) Reissued Jianghai Customs 2.5% Surtax National Treasury Bonds: Interest has been paid in 24 installments. (3) Tobacco Tax National Treasury Bonds: Principal and interest have been paid up to the 21st installment. (4) Post-Rehabilitation Short-Term Public Bonds: Principal and interest have been redeemed three times. (5) 1928 Financial Short-Term Public Bonds: Principal and interest have been redeemed twice. (6) 1928 Financial Long-Term Public Bonds: Interest has been paid twice. (7) 1929 Disaster Relief Public Bonds: Principal and interest have been redeemed twice. (8) 1929 Troop Reduction Public Bonds: Principal and interest have been redeemed twice. (9) Reissued Tobacco Tax National Treasury Bonds: Principal and interest have been paid in nine installments. (10) 1929 Customs Duty Treasury Bonds: Principal and interest have been paid in seven installments. (11) 1929 Demobilization Treasury Bonds: Principal and interest have been paid in four installments.
