Free Talk

To Be Dismissed with a Laugh

— Hai Ke

Judge (to the criminal): Why did you only take the money bag and not the silver utensils next to it?

Criminal: Only because the basket was too heavy.

Judge: So lazy. Aren't you ashamed of yourself?

Female A: This time, I finally got back at the editor of the newspaper who rejected my manuscript.

Female B: How did you get back at him?

Female A: His son proposed to me. And I rejected him.

Shop assistant: The owner summoned me. I wonder what instructions he has.

Shop owner: I'm going to fire you at the end of the month. But my memory is very bad. Please remind me then.

Painter: General. I have finished two-thirds of your portrait. It's almost done.

General: This painting doesn't need to be painted anymore. You have to paint another one. Because I have been promoted to division commander.

Diner: The steak I ate here yesterday was much bigger than today's.

Waiter: Yes, sir. Because today's steak is cut from a calf.

Orchid Cause Buried with a Boat Girl

— Yingchuan Furun

The mountains and rivers of Zhejiang are the best in the world. The spiritual beauty is concentrated there, and beautiful women are produced. Boat girl Liu Gehong is a small family's gem. Her ancestors were a prominent clan in Tongjiang, with a reputation for officialdom. However, the girl's father was addicted to gambling, gambling day and night, and the family was ruined. Unable to make a living, he urged his daughter to go north to Fuchun to carry passengers by boat to earn a meager living. The girl's beauty was unparalleled, and her charm was outstanding. Her bright eyes stirred people's emotions with every turn. Those who were quick to lust for her vied for her attention. There was a scholar named Ding from Hulin, a gentle and handsome young man. Last spring, he came to Fu to assist in village administration by order of the Department of Civil Affairs. Because he was not familiar with the place, he went to the ferry to find a boat and met the girl. He was surprised by her celestial beauty, and his soul was given to her. He bowed down before her. When he tried to speak to her, her words and demeanor were like pearls, beautiful and fluent, like a yellow oriole singing out of the valley. They fell in love with each other and regretted meeting so late. From then on, they enjoyed the early spring flowers and the autumn moon. They often shared a small boat, swaying on the Fuchun River, in perfect harmony, envied by the two mandarin ducks sleeping on the sand.

From spring to summer to autumn to winter, the scholar suffered from anemia. He lingered for several months, and the girl worked tirelessly to care for him. But heaven did not bless them. He could not recover from his illness and died one night during a strong wind and bitter rain. The girl also drank a knife beside him that night, becoming a martyr for the sake of their love. Alas. Ding's friends planned to bury them together on the east side of Dongshan and have already contacted both families to finalize this beautiful tale.

A Record of the Zhongshan Park in Guangzhou

— Lü Bing

A guest from Guangzhou talked extensively about the affairs of Guangzhou. Guangzhou is the most prosperous metropolis in the southern part of our country. In recent years, it has strived to modernize its city administration. The roads have been widened, and the streets are clean. It is truly the crown of the Southeast. Guangzhou City has Zhongshan Park, which occupies several acres of land. The layout is very beautiful. Flowers, trees, pavilions, and ponds are all available. It is a great place for citizens to play and relax. The municipal government strives to improve it, using public entertainment venues to promote its policies. Each pavilion in the park is equipped with a sound transmission tube. Wireless broadcasts are aired from one to five in the afternoon. Visitors gather, and all kinds of reports from various speakers, market conditions, celebrity speeches, and famous singers are heard clearly in the valley. Western music is also played occasionally. Foreigners who visit this garden often borrow a patch of greenery.

Literary Tiger Guessing

— Wu Lianzhou

Literary tiger. A game for literary people. In recent years, the study of traditional Chinese learning has declined, almost to the point of becoming extinct. Little does one know that the literary tiger can promote the arts, assist in education, and cultivate good leisure habits. I have written dozens of riddles with Sun Yusheng, Cao Qionghan, Shi Jiqun, and Zhang Haiyun. They will be published in this column daily. If you wish to guess, please mail your answers within three days to my medical residence next to the Shen Bao newspaper office on Sanma Road. A small reward is prepared to encourage your refined interest.

This year's Literary Tiger Night 1. Opera name: Green smoke covers the sound of spring... Performer's name: A spring breeze and a new tune... Six-character sentence: Smiling, she asks someone else to adjust her crown... Kun opera name: The winding patterns rotate, with chanting of scriptures... Common saying: The golden bridle horse neighs on the fragrant grassland... Road name: Accumulated snow melts away, revealing the bones of the mountain... Medicine name: Pestle enters Qiantang, in the Yangzi... Character: (Cao Shuheng's excellent work will continue tomorrow)

Holding hands in the ancient Tango dance adds color to the beautiful garden. Although there are many famous gardens in Shanghai, such equipment is not yet heard of. And Guangzhou has uniquely opened the trend first. The guest said it like that. I will bring it up, so that people in Shanghai or something may be a lesson.

Beauty Drinking Games

— Dan Dang Sheng

Li's Green Cloud Mountain House faces a stream with a bamboo forest surrounding it. Colleagues gathered there for a winter meeting. They always used elegant songs to accompany the wine. By the sixth meeting, they decided to slightly change the previous practice. Lin Jun Heqing said, "I have an idea, which can be called the Beauty Drinking Game. Write words related to the human body on paper rolls, such as beauty's heart, beauty's eyes, beauty's mouth, etc. Everything on a beauty's body can be written on them, so we can get dozens of rolls. The method of ordering is to draw a roll and see what word is on it. Then, use this word to lead into an idiom and recite it. And let one person sitting in the order to drink serve as the order official. If the idiom contains this word, then count from yourself to the number of the word. That is, the number of people to drink. This is straightforward and does not require an order official. The reason why an order official is needed is that the idiom quoted may only cut the meaning of the word, and does not see the literal meaning, then the order official judges. Who should drink? The judgment must have a reason. If the person who should drink does not accept the judgment, and the reasoning is smoother, the order official cannot yield, then the order official drinks himself. Lin Jun then gave an example to the people sitting with him and said, "For example, if you draw a roll for beauty's eyes, recite it, 'Beautiful eyes look forward,' then the second person drinks. The second person is the order official, and should not refuse. Or recite, 'Want to see the distant horizon,' then the fifth person drinks. This sentence does not cut beauty, but it can be flexible. If the public thinks that it should be strict, then the person who should order for all the sentences quoted must accompany a cup. Or recite, 'How can he endure the autumn waves of that turn when he leaves,' This only cuts the meaning of the word, and does not see the literal meaning, then the order official can judge it and say, 'The word autumn wave is in six or seven, and the sixth and seventh people sitting in the row drink.' And Zhang Xing, who is sitting in the middle, should also drink. It is because of this turn of autumn wave, which is for Zhang Junrui. Only autumn wave is still focused on the word. If you encounter a sentence that is completely written in general, the order official will have a lot of thoughts." So everyone praised him. Immediately, they cut paper to make rolls and took a pen to write. They searched for words for the beauty's body, even the intestines, stomach, lungs, and liver, where they could not be seen. Also written into the rolls. There are even some obscene ones, and nothing is left out. Breaking three characters into four characters, such as fingernails and body hair, etc., is meticulous. After writing, there are forty-two rolls. Once the order is carried out, beautiful thoughts, beautiful words, jade crumbs, and clear words, laughter, and confusion, and exchanges are crossed, it can be said that the joy of drinking is exhausted. The following is a record of the order official's judgment that is more interesting. Yang Jun Weiruru drew beauty's tears. Because he recited, "Falling to the autumn steps, sea begonias grow." The order official Li Haichou said, "Weiruru and I were classmates in childhood. Knowing his nickname is Qiu Tang, he should drink two cups." Weiruru said, "I intended to shoot you with the word sea, but I am punishing myself." Haichou said, "I can have one cup, and you should double it." Zhang Jun Zhonghua drew a beauty's arm. He recited, "Who can dispel the jade bend on the pillow." I was the order official and said, "Wang Jun Zhuoru drinks." Asked why, he said, "You initiated the Winter Cooling Society. The jade quality is cold and cold. You are the master of the Winter Cooling Society, and colleagues should let you enjoy this beautiful blessing." Li Jun Haichou drew a beauty's hand. He recited, "I iron my fingers for my husband." The order official said, "Please ask Zhuoru to drink again." Asked why, he said, "This is also the beauty that the master of the Winter Cooling Society enjoys alone." And this sentence is Wang Cihui's poem. You are surnamed Wang. There is also a relationship. Because your drinking capacity is not large, otherwise, you should offer two cups." I drew a beauty's private. Searching for a long time, it was difficult to get it immediately. First of all, Wang Jun Yunsheng had already drawn this and recited the sentence "No one speaks privately at midnight." Although the word "private" is clearly embedded, it is not precise. The order official said that in addition to the fifth person drinking, he ruled that the person sitting side by side on the left should drink. It is said that he had watched the Palace of Eternal Life.

Red Felt

Xun Huisheng Discusses Drama

— Wei

I wrote a previous discussion on Huisheng's performance of the play "Thirteenth Sister". The opening performance was crowded. Watching the entire play, it was tightly connected and the performance was full of highlights. The postures and movements up and down the stage all contained chivalry in their charm. There were several fast-paced and original-paced segments of singing. The intonation was also clear, stable, gentle, and harmonious. It had been performed before at the Yuelaidian in Hongliucun and Nengren Temple. This time, the redundant scenes were removed, while the key points were retained. For example, the section of returning to the store from Yuelaidian has now been deleted, because the passage of the donkey driver has no particular meaning. The recitations were clear, word by word. Saving Zhang An and his wife and accomplishing a good deed can overwhelm his peers in terms of vividness. Changing into plain clothes to keep vigil further revealed his eagerness for revenge between his eyebrows. It was not until he met Zhang Jinfeng, who proposed marriage, that he realized there was an opportunity to fulfill a beautiful dream together. He was extremely wonderful when embarrassed by Zhang. The final scene of capturing the thief, although a small wave, also concluded the entire play. The story of this play is found in the novels, with Furong Cao and Zhang Jinfeng. The Zhuzhu all called the father and son of Chunyan Zhongren's family. The wife of the Fulu monk, her every move and speech, made people recognize her as handsome. Cao Mao, Bao Deng Jiu Gong, was also very diligent.

The play "Du Shiniang Angrily Sinks the Treasure Chest" had almost become a play that no one in the southern female roles did not perform in the past. Among the average actors, there has not yet been a performance. Huisheng and the famous playwright Mr. Chen Moxiang revised this book, adding singing lyrics. The melody is elegant and acceptable. The singing style is also different from others. Su San Yaxian... the performance has already gained public praise. Ten Niang must be able to do the same.

People only know that Huisheng is best at playing Huadan, but they don't know that she can perform tragic and mournful plays. In Ping, there are two plays written: "Yuzaogong, Queen Lu Jealousy Slaying Consort Qi," and "Lu Fangweng's Xiu Zi's Hairpin Phoenix". Every time they are performed, no one in the audience can help but shed tears due to emotional impact. The script is perfect and beneficial to the world.

On Xu Biyun

— Hao

Generally, to become a famous actor, one must have the basic advantages that make them famous. I usually don't like watching plays, but I especially like listening to the radio. During my rest, I occasionally use this as a pastime. I find that the records of Qingyi are the most pleasant to listen to, because they are quiet, delicate, and graceful. And Xu Biyun's "Baolian Lantern", "Imperial Stele Pavilion", "Yutang Chun", and other plays are especially clear and fluent. From this, I know that her fame cannot be achieved by luck. Biyun is an outstanding talent from Binqing Society. She has come to Shanghai several times, and her reputation is comparable to that of the Four Vajras. I occasionally go to listen to her plays. I feel that her voice has reached the point of perfection, and her expressions and recitations are especially like Mei Lanfang. I know that she is deeply influenced by him. In the future, she will follow Wanhua and rise, and she is the one. Biyun's masterpiece "Yutang Chun" has been sold out many times. There are also dramas such as "The Pearl Dream" and "Farewell to Green Pearl," which will be performed in sequence. There should be another grand occasion.

The secret oath of the Qixi Festival, Tang Minghuang was always on the left side of the noble concubine. I thought about it for a while, and then said, "I have a saying from the emperor." Everyone asked what it was. I said, "Woman is a tool." Someone said, "Is this also a jieduling?" I said, "Yes. The character 'Ru' is often written as the character 'Nu' in ancient books." Someone asked, "Are all organs called tools? I'm afraid it's difficult to pinpoint the character for 'private.'" I smiled. The order official Wang Jun said, "The word 'also' is written as 'female yin' in the Shuowen Jiezi. This sentence can be said to be extremely precise." Then he pointed at Yu Jun and said, "You should drink. What tool is asked below? It's a coral." There is a character 'coral' in your name, so you should drink." I remember that Suiyuan's poetry says that you need to use a beauty soldier for winter cooling. Such a drinking order can also be called a winter cooling story.

Record of a Banquet at the Small Bottle Flower Studio

— Yan Xiaxiang Ke

The day after the Lantern Festival was clear, and the spring was still cold. The owner of the Small Bottle Flower Studio hosted a banquet, and the guests were all noble and refined companions, hiding their tracks by the sea, each supporting themselves with their writings, paintings, and calligraphy, without making money in the mundane world. Halfway through the wine, the host took out his collection of famous paintings, screens, hand scrolls, fan albums, and other things from ancient and modern times, one by one. Mr. Tang Dongfu has not been selling paintings for long, and I didn't know him. On this day, I saw one of his four-foot scrolls and two of his paintings on fans. I felt that his intentions were lofty and far-reaching, and his brushstrokes were deep and elegant. He was able to combine the styles of Shi Tian, ​​Mo Jing, and Lianzhou. I asked the owner, and I learned that Mr. Tang was a direct descendant of Tang Zhenmin, General Yusheng. It is appropriate that his family has a long history of learning and is far from ordinary. He can be compared with Mr. Gu Wu and others in recent days. I heard that Mr. Tang is humble and upright. He neither follows the crowd nor creates differences. Outside of painting, he is also fond of cups and handles. I am also a drunkard. Although I know a little about painting, I dare not get involved. The owner loves painting but refuses to paint himself. His collection is extremely rich, and his appraisal is especially precise. Now that I have seen Mr. Tang's paintings for the first time, and they have been obtained by the owner, I am even more impressed by his ability to have a discerning eye. So I raised a large white cup to congratulate the owner and retreated to write a record for him and Mr. Tang, and made friends with them. (Pay back)

European Travel Newsletter (40)

— Liu Haisu

Bourdelle's Death LamortdeBourdelle

㈠ Bad news

September 20th. We finished our two-month trip. Returned to Paris from Switzerland. At this time, my most urgent task. That is to send my wife to school to study. Tiger followed Liu Kang to Fontainebleau on September 28th to attend middle school. Then Yunshi was introduced by Ms. Cheng Qieying. To a girls' school in Bezon, 50 miles near Paris.

On the afternoon of October 2nd. I sent Yunshi to Baicong with Mr. Chuan Lei Zhang Xian. We took the car. Keep walking, keep walking. Exit Paris city. Walking through several large bridges. The rapid Seine and Marna rivers are lined with jagged tree trunks. The clear, deep autumn sunlight is flooded on the tops of the branches. When the long car ride ended. Approaching our destination Beano. Feels very comfortable.

At the end of the tramway. Quiet and lonely. All of them are corners of country-style streets. It is a simple brick building surrounded by wooden fences. Probably exposed to years of wind and rain. It has become a quaint dark gray. Both doors are tightly closed. No one was seen silently. A horizontal plaque is embedded above. Inscribed in gold with PensiounagNotregDame

It wasn't long. We went to ring the doorbell.

As soon as the door opened. It is a large flower garden. Most trees like oak trees. Casts small shadows. Projected on the green lawn. We explained our intentions to the porter. Led into the living room on the right. After waiting for a while. The principal came out. Wearing a black dress. Is an old man who seems to be over sixty years old. Whitened temples. Short stature. Showing a gentle appearance like an old virgin.

We first stated our intentions. She then said. The room has already been prepared. Miss Zheng and Mrs. Wang have been here for many years. Is this MadameLiu? Very young. She said these words. I then paid the tuition. Yunshi's luggage was moved into the dormitory. The dormitory is on the north side of the courtyard. There are a dozen simple and clean rooms. Divided between female students. Quietly like a monastery. Yun occupied one of the small houses. At that time, Yun Shi looked quite happy and lively. It was dusk. We then said goodbye to the principal and Yunshi. Left this school.

Flourishing Foreign Exchange Market Reflects Economic Vitality

Market Overview: The period of silver dollar expansion has not yet arrived, and the money market is still limited to single transactions. There is no sign of a vigorous trend. However, yesterday, due to the enthusiastic trading of foreign currency by banks, and the transactions among brokers, the market was quite active, and the situation yesterday morning was no less vibrant than usual. However, observing the trading scene, supply exceeded demand, leading to a slight decrease in prices. As for the future of silver discounts, they remained as loose as before, so there was no market trend worth noting.

Discount Rates: Selling pressure was quite strong for longer terms, and discount rates opened low, but were then pulled up by both sides, eventually ending up similar to the previous day, only slightly lower by two hao and a half, at seven qian, one fen, eight li, one hao, and two hu and a half. There was no market price before the morning market started. The silver discount morning market, transfer, and other market conditions all opened with white borrowing. The afternoon small general meeting was the only exception, also operating on a borrowing basis. Bank rates and premium head money were still not quoted.

Subsidiary Coin Market: Jiangnan small foreign coins mostly trended towards stability, weakening again by seven hao and a half yesterday morning to six qian and four fen, similar to Monday's market price. Only two thousand five hundred jiao were traded. Guangdong small foreign coins continued to decline, reaching five qian, nine fen, and five li yesterday, lower by two li compared to the previous day's low. One hundred twenty-five thousand jiao were traded. Discount exchange rates increased by four jiao, reaching one thousand two hundred and seven jiao. Copper coins continued to rise by one thousand wen, totaling four hundred and eleven thousand wen. A large number of transactions were made, totaling over forty-nine thousand strings. Silver Dollar Inflow and Outflow: The amount of silver received and remitted by banks in the market yesterday was slightly more than before. South and North Goods Dried Longan Industry Wildly Raises Market Price

Arising from Sample Deduction Dispute

The dried longan industry's spring market opening has not yet commenced due to new demands for 98% or 99% sample deductions. However, various firms believe this demand greatly affects the owners of the goods and must seek agreement from peers and owners before responding and deciding on a method. Thus, the trade association is impatient, using the refusal to open trading as leverage, and is wildly raising market prices at other firms. For example, top-grade large round longans, selected by experts, of superior yellow color, were only selling for thirty-one or thirty-two taels. However, yesterday, the original customer goods were raised to thirty-four taels, leading to inverted costs and unstable market conditions. However, through this rise, the market trend has indeed tightened, and it may turn false into reality and become a normal market; one cannot say for sure.

Prediction of Red Plate for Oil Market Hankow Oil

The red plate for Hankou oil is the latest. In the past, the opening of the market in the second month of the lunar calendar was common. In the last ten years, the market has opened after the Lantern Festival. The reason is that the number of borrowed loading facilities has gradually decreased year by year, and market fluctuations are uncertain, so it is better to open early to set the price of borrowed oil. Now that the Lantern Festival is near, the red plate is said to be under discussion. According to news, it will be announced within two or three days. It is said that it will be roughly the same as the end of the year. Ren Zhongjing is predicted to be thirteen taels and two mace, San Heng thirteen taels and eight mace, miscellaneous heavy twelve taels, Ping Jing twelve taels and four or five mace, Tianjin city twelve taels two or three mace to twelve taels. However, Macheng oil must be twelve taels and eight mace, which seems better, because a few foreign firms have handled it. The estimated gross village goods are thirteen taels. Although the number is not large, it does not lack embellishment on the market. Although this is a predicted plate, it will not deviate too much. According to detailed letters, the red plate opening price in Jinhua and Lanxi and other places is plus one. Duzhu alone is sixteen yuan and eight jiao, Ming Jian sixteen yuan and four jiao, Zhengan sixteen yuan, and De Gan fifteen yuan and eight jiao, which seems to be an improvement over last year. However, it is also the scene that the red plate should have. A letter from Hangzhou dealers reports that the inner ping oil is twenty-one yuan and four jiao, and various banks sent friends to Shanghai to sell for twenty yuan and eight jiao, which shows that the reported price and the selling price are inconsistent, and the difference between visiting customers and selling goods. There have been no customers for the local car oil in Jiaxing, but it is said that the inland selling price is twenty-one yuan and four or five jiao per car, while sending to Shanghai is still between twenty-one yuan and seven or eight jiao.

Silk and Tea Chinese Silk Must Have Inspection Certificate to be Exported

Implemented on March 1... The Ministry of Industry and Commerce has sent a letter to the Jianghai Customs for verification. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce, in order to develop the European sales of Chinese silk, specifically ordered the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau to establish a raw silk inspection office, which will be implemented on March 1. After that, regardless of whether the factory white, yellow, or gray silk is transported to European and American countries, an inspection certificate issued by the raw silk inspection office must be presented before the customs will allow it to pass. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce yesterday sent a letter to the Jianghai Customs to verify and implement it.

Yellow and White Factory Silk Goods are Scarce and Prices are Firm

Yesterday, the foreign firms' silk market showed even greater prosperity. The European and American markets need raw silk due to spring goods, and the Shanghai port frequently sends telegrams to transfer to Shanghai. Due to the scarcity of raw materials and insufficient remaining goods, the market atmosphere is even firmer for Chinese silk merchants. Yesterday, ten packages of Shanghai white factory silk were imported by the public security, etc. The price of silk was firm and popular.

Those who live in their own houses will also add some decorations to enhance the appearance and avoid being ridiculed for being inferior. However, large landlords are not like this. In their minds, they only pursue the lowest cost and the highest income.

In the past, residential areas in Shanghai were all limited to the public concession. After tenants rented a house, they often installed their own bathtubs, washbasins, kitchen utensils, gas pipes, electric lights, etc. When moving, they would dismantle and take away these decorations, which caused great losses to themselves, and the houses were damaged by excavation, and the cost of redecoration by the new tenants was not available. Moreover, in the past, if you wanted to get hot water, you could either get it from the kitchen, or cook it yourself in a large pot, or get it from the so-called tiger stove nearby. How could there be the convenience of today's hot and cold water pipes? In the past, landlords never asked about the improvement and decoration of houses, etc., and tenants were not willing to spend a lot of money on properties that did not belong to them, except for the necessities.

This company has made great contributions to the various improvements and advantages of today's new and beautiful residences in Shanghai.

The goal of this company is to improve the living conditions in Shanghai and encourage tenants to become owners of their own houses. This company has chosen undeveloped plots with careful eyes and clear foresight, and has obtained the cooperation of the authorities, and has engaged in opening up roads, dividing land, and building various beautiful houses with different styles on it, which has revolutionized the rough brick house atmosphere of the past. The houses built by the China Business Company have different styles, and the most modern decorations in the room, the family members who live in it, are especially admired. Such as sanitary equipment, such as kitchen bathrooms, etc., all four walls are paved with magnetic tiles, large magnetic basins, bathtubs, hot and cold water pipes, gas pipes, electric pipes, flushing toilets, etc., everything is available and strives for excellence.

About fifteen years ago, there was a large square of farmland between Da Hualong Road, Jin Shenfu Road, Lafayette Road, and the French Park, and its price was only between 1,000 and 1,500 taels per mu. This company saw this and purchased the land from various small owners, and the plan was immediately started. The French Concession Public Works Bureau knew that the company's plan was of great benefit to the concession and did its best to help, such as gas, tap water, electricity, and other utilities, all of which have been deeply cooperated, especially the widening of roads and the planting of trees on sidewalks.

The company's plan has been very effective. However, the company does not take the land as its own for profit, but divides the land into several small squares and sells it for 2,000 taels per mu.

Some of the houses are sold for cash after they are built. It is also possible to mortgage loans or pay monthly payments in lieu of rent without cash. Moreover, if the residents are dissatisfied with this type of house, the company can also advance funds to build a new house to their liking. The conditions for selling houses can not only encourage savings, but also force frugality, which is one of the most beneficial investments.

In today's Shanghai, this section is not the most superior residential area, but also one of the most superior residential areas. There is no vacant land in it, and all homeowners are owners of their own houses. The value of this land is estimated at about 15,000 taels per mu at the current land price, and the houses can be sold for 40,000 to 60,000 taels per house.

All those who purchase real estate according to this company's method not only live in extreme comfort, but also save and become rich, or sell and obtain huge profits.

The Chinese people today need housing improvement. However, before today, the Chinese middle class really had no opportunity to buy Chinese-style houses. Therefore, the houses they lived in were all purchased by large landlords, and large landlords only looked at profit. The more buildings, the greater the income, the lighter the construction cost, and the greater the profit. Therefore, those who live in these houses can hardly be called a family, and can only be called a place to shelter from the wind and rain. Moreover, the rent is extremely high. An ordinary property only has a general deed.

The China Business Company firmly believes that the Chinese people, especially women, all want their own houses, which can be occupied exclusively for themselves and can be arbitrarily added, modified, or decorated. This company has seen this and wants to make a test to prove this ideal, so it is engaged in building a large section of Chinese-style houses again. Each house is equipped with various modern devices, and the rest is divided into several squares, each square has a separate deed. Once the houses there are built, they can be sold, or purchased with cash, or other conditions can be agreed, all of which are possible.

All those who purchase real estate, whose plans and policies are adapted to the needs of society, also help the development of that society the most. Therefore, one hundred small owners are more beneficial to society than one large owner.

This company also has a so-called real estate mortgage mutual benefit bond, that is, small savers can enjoy the same preferential interest as large savers. The company accepts savings of 10 taels or 10 yuan or more, and pays interest at 7%, which is paid twice every six months. This type of savings is invested by the company in mortgages of the best real estate, and is specifically used to guarantee this type of bond separately. In addition, the company uses the company's entire assets as collateral. The company has established a special department to manage this matter separately. 25% of the interest on this type of bond is used as a dividend, so the annual interest on holding this type of bond is always at 8% or more, which was the case for the past four years.

The most reliable and most effective business is the real estate trust company, and its financial position in real estate is like a bank in commerce. All societies, regardless of size, in which companies with real estate as their business, are based on the number of their people and the amount of real estate investment.

The real estate investment in Shanghai is unknown how many tens of millions, but the people of Shanghai still do not have a publicly recognized place where they can borrow cash with reliable collateral (real estate title deeds), and real estate sales can be completed quickly. New buyers can thus obtain information on various needs for consideration, and sellers can know the current value of their real estate at any time and compare it with the value of real estate around them. They can obtain economic assistance, so that construction can be well improved, and mortgage savings and other items can be quickly found to eliminate the delays of various large real estate companies in demanding guarantees and insurance.

The China Business Company is planning to issue all of its 1.5 million taels of unissued shares, increasing the share capital to 2 million taels. Then, it will engage in organizing a large-scale real estate trust company. Since its establishment, this company has been in business for more than 20 years, and its management personnel and business policies have not changed from beginning to end. Therefore, all those who have transactions with this company, whether Chinese or foreign, have expressed satisfaction, and this company has been able to carefully study the real estate business in Shanghai and make the business progress day by day. The mortgage loans handled by this company have reached no less than 45 million taels of principal and interest, all of which have been fully paid off, which is clear evidence. The location of the China Business Company is in the center of Shanghai's business and also the gathering point of Shanghai's real estate business. There are more than 90 Chinese and foreign employees, and it manages more than 5,000 houses. There are as many as 800 people involved in the trust of Chinese real estate. The greatness of the company's productivity, the breadth of its vision, and the effectiveness of its management can be seen in its announced business situation.
